Program support is provided on musescore.org.\r\n\r\n\r\nFeatures supported by MuseScore include:\r\n\r\n* Unlimited score length\r\n* Unlimited number of staves per system\r\n* Up to four independent voices per staff\r\n* Score creation wizard and templates\r\n* Guitar, bass, ukulele, lute tablature\r\n* Automatic part extraction and transposition\r\n* Repeats, including segnos, codas, and measure repeats\r\n* Dynamics, articulations, and other expression markings, with playback support for most\r\n* Custom text markings\r\n* Lyrics\r\n* Chord symbols\r\n* Jazz notation, including lead sheets, slash notation and a ‚Äúhandwritten‚Äù font for text\r\n* Swing and shuffle playback\r\n* Mixer for instrument levels and effects\r\n* Percussion notation\r\n* Early music notation\r\n* Cross-staff beaming\r\n* Import of graphics\r\n* Custom key signatures\r\n* Additive time signatures\r\n* User-defined score styles\r\n\r\nMost elements in MuseScore are laid out automatically but can also be positioned manually. The capabilities of MuseScore can be extended via plugins, and the growing repository on musescore.org contains many plugins submitted by users.\r\n\r\nMuseScore includes a set of sounds that reproduce common instruments (as defined by General MIDI) without taking up a lot of disk space or memory, but you can also substitute any SoundFont you prefer for a wider variety of sounds or for more realism.\r\n\r\nMuseScore can import and export MIDI and MusicXML files, and it can also import from Capella and several other programs. MuseScore can export to PDF, PNG, and other graphic formats, to WAV and other audio formats, or to Lilypond for an alternative layout and print In addition, the deck contains four each of \"Wild\" and \"Wild Draw Four\" cards\r\n\r\nEach player is dealt 7 cards and the remaining cards are placed face down to form a draw pile. \r\nThe first player has to match the card in the discard pile either by number or color or the player can throw down a Wild Card else he must pick a card from the draw pile. If he can play what is drawn, great. Otherwise play moves to the next person.\r\n\r\nIn Uno The card deck contains four colors with numbers from 0 to 9, as well as Action cards - \"Reverse\", \"Skip\", \"Take Two\", \"Wild\" and \"Wild Take Four\".\r\n\r\nThe winner is first one who has no cards left. \r\n\r\nNow you can play Uno Classic with your Facebook friends, against the computer or with millions of Uno players around the world.\r\n\r\nYou can also create a Private Room and invite your friends to play.\r\n\r\nThe biggest advantage of Uno Classic card game is that it can be enjoyed by everybody in the family.
